        }
        mr-issue-page[issueClosed] {
          --monorail-metadata-toggled-bg: var(--monorail-metadata-closed-bg);
        }
        mr-issue-page[codeFont] {
          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }
        .container-issue {
          width: 100%;
          flex-direction: column;
          align-items: stretch;
          justify-content: flex-start;
          z-index: 200;
        }
        .container-issue-content {
          padding: 0;
          flex-grow: 1;
          display: flex;
          align-items: stretch;
          justify-content: space-between;
          flex-direction: row;

          box-sizing: border-box;
          padding-top: 0.5em;
        }
        .container-outside {
          box-sizing: border-box;
          width: 100%;
          max-width: 100%;
          margin: auto;
          padding: 0;
          display: flex;
          align-items: stretch;
          justify-content: space-between;
          flex-direction: row;
          flex-wrap: no-wrap;
        }
        .container-no-issue {
          padding: 0.5em 16px;
          font-size: var(--chops-large-font-size);
        }
        .metadata-container {
          font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
          background: var(--monorail-metadata-toggled-bg);
          border-right: var(--chops-normal-border);

          width: 24em;
          min-width: 256px;
          flex-grow: 0;
          flex-shrink: 0;
          box-sizing: border-box;
          z-index: 100;
        }
        .issue-header-container {
          z-index: 10;
          position: sticky;
          top: var(--monorail-header-height);
          margin-bottom: 0.25em;
          width: 100%;
        }
        mr-issue-details {
          min-width: 50%;
          max-width: 1000px;
          flex-grow: 1;
          box-sizing: border-box;
          min-height: 100%;

          padding-right: var(--mr-issue-page-horizontal-padding);
        }
        mr-issue-metadata {
          position: sticky;
          overflow-y: auto;
          top: var(--monorail-header-height);
          height: calc(100vh - var(--monorail-header-height));
        }
        mr-launch-overview {
          border-left: var(--chops-normal-border);

            padding: 0 var(--mr-issue-page-horizontal-padding);
          }
          mr-issue-details, mr-launch-overview {
            width: 100%;
            padding: 0;

        @media (max-width: 840px) {

          }
        }

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        <p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

<b class="line"><!---->VULNERABILITY DETAILS<!----></b>



<br>





Hello, I found this bug via fuzzing. It leads to the following CHECK:



<span class="line"><!---->Hello, I found this bug via fuzzing. It leads to the following CHECK:<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





# Fatal error in gen/torque-generated/src/objects/struct-tq-inl.inc, line 4



<span class="line"><!----># Fatal error in gen/torque-generated/src/objects/struct-tq-inl.inc, line 4<!----></span>



<br>





# Check failed: !v8::internal::FLAG_enable_slow_asserts || (IsStruct_NonInline(*this)).



<span class="line"><!----># Check failed: !v8::internal::FLAG_enable_slow_asserts || (IsStruct_NonInline(*this)).<!----></span>



<br>



<br>



<br>



<br>





VERSION



<b class="line"><!---->VERSION<!----></b>



<br>





I verified this crash in v8 version v8 9.4.0 (commit hash: 



<span class="line"><!---->I verified this crash in v8 version v8 9.4.0 (commit hash: <!----></span>





185badc9122fe6274c1b2fe54e03fda5315cb80e



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://crrev.com/185badc9122fe6274c1b2fe54e03fda5315cb80e"><!---->185badc9122fe6274c1b2fe54e03fda5315cb80e<!----></a>





)



<span class="line"><!---->)<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





I compiled it using:



<span class="line"><!---->I compiled it using:<!----></span>



<br>





gn gen out/fuzzbuild --args='is_debug=true dcheck_always_on=true v8_static_library=true v8_enable_slow_dchecks=true v8_enable_v8_checks=true v8_enable_verify_heap=true v8_enable_verify_csa=true v8_fuzzilli=true v8_enable_verify_predictable=true target_cpu="x64"'



<span class="line"><!---->gn gen out/fuzzbuild --args='is_debug=true dcheck_always_on=true v8_static_library=true v8_enable_slow_dchecks=true v8_enable_v8_checks=true v8_enable_verify_heap=true v8_enable_verify_csa=true v8_fuzzilli=true v8_enable_verify_predictable=true target_cpu="x64"'<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





And I started d8 with the following flag:



<span class="line"><!---->And I started d8 with the following flag:<!----></span>



<br>





./d8 --interrupt-budget=1024 /path/to/crash.js



<span class="line"><!---->./d8 --interrupt-budget=1024 /path/to/crash.js<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





The "--interrupt-budget=1024" flag is important to trigger the CHECK.



<span class="line"><!---->The "--interrupt-budget=1024" flag is important to trigger the CHECK.<!----></span>

In



<span class="line"><!---->In<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





 script = handle(Script::cast(script->eval_from_shared().script()), isolate);



<span class="line"><!----> script = handle(Script::cast(script-&gt;eval_from_shared().script()), isolate);<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





`script->eval_from_shared().script()` may be `undefined`, i.e. not a Script. A quick change to fix the potential security issue is to add a `CHECK(script->eval_from_shared().script().IsScript())`.



<span class="line"><!---->`script-&gt;eval_from_shared().script()` may be `undefined`, i.e. not a Script. A quick change to fix the potential security issue is to add a `CHECK(script-&gt;eval_from_shared().script().IsScript())`.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:v8/src/runtime/runtime-module.cc;l=31;drc=068d917a72636ddbb64dfa7ecabe6bac71bd4b26



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:v8/src/runtime/runtime-module.cc;l=31;drc=068d917a72636ddbb64dfa7ecabe6bac71bd4b26"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:v8/src/runtime/runtime-module.cc;l=31;drc=068d917a72636ddbb64dfa7ecabe6bac71bd4b26<!----></a>

<span class="line"><!---->We see that frames 1 and 2 from the --noopt case are not present in the --opt case.<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->In the unoptimized version, `find` has its own frame which is filtered out by `return js_frame-&gt;function().shared().IsSubjectToDebugging();`: <!----></span>





https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:v8/src/execution/frames.cc;l=213;drc=0ce9df69ba9e32bafc53c3d90db8a707c243da40



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:v8/src/execution/frames.cc;l=213;drc=0ce9df69ba9e32bafc53c3d90db8a707c243da40"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:v8/src/execution/frames.cc;l=213;drc=0ce9df69ba9e32bafc53c3d90db8a707c243da40<!----></a>





.

*** Boilerplate reminders! ***



<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.



<span class="line"><!---->Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.<!----></span>
